FNV MATERIAL TEXTURE SLOT LAYOUT FOLLOWUP AUDIT

Questions:
1. What is BSShaderPPLighting object field +0xDC (param_1[0x37])?
2. What does that object's +0x6C gate represent before pass IDs 4/5?
3. Which functions map diffuse/normal/bump/glow/gloss/dark/decal source slots to draw-time bindings?
4. Can Psycho safely attach roughness/metalness conventions without trusting 0x011F91E0 outside the draw path?
